# ============================================================================
# CHAOS REDUX - EVENT 005 SOVIET COLLAPSE REPUBLIC FOCUS TREES
# ============================================================================
# Runtime trees for event-created republics. Ukraine, Belarus, Kazakhstan, and
# the shared emergency fallback have clean-spec replacement trees; remaining
# regional trees still use compact country packages until their own replacement
# slices land.
# ============================================================================
